INC-SOURCE (D-T) Less than 2 nsec pulsed neutrons were generated  22278  1   18 
            at a repetition rate of 0.5 MHz. The angular distribu-22278  1   19 
            tion of the source neutron yield was known to within  22278  1   20 
            2.4% from Al foil activation measurements.            22278  1   21 
SAMPLE      Cylinder geometry. The size of the scattering samples 22278  1   22 
            was 3.0 cm in diameter and 7.0 cm in length.          22278  1   23 
            Samples placed at 17 cm point                         22278  1   24 
METHOD     (TOF)   Neutron flight path length was about 8.3 m.    22278  1   25 
           (ACTIV) The angular distribution of the source neutron 22278  1   26 
                   yield measurements.                            22278  1   27 
DETECTOR   (SCIN)  NE-213 liquid scintillator 25.4 cm in diameter 22278  1   28 
            and 10.0 cm in length. The detector was shielded from 22278  1   29 
            source and room scattered neutrons, a shadowbar       22278  1   30 
            and different collimators. The source neutron flux was22278  1   31 
            monitored by another NE213 scintillator with 5.08 cm  22278  1   32 
            diameter and 5.08 cm length, which was set at zero    22278  1   33 
            degrees with respect to the deuteron beam line.       22278  1   34 
MONITOR    (1-H-1(N,EL)1-H-1,,DA)                                 22278  1   35 
CORRECTION  Corrections are made for                              22278  1   36 
             - multiple scattering;                               22278  1   37 
             - attenuation;                                       22278  1   38 
             - neutron source contamination.                      22278  1   39 
            based on JENDL-3. In case that JENDL-3 would produce  22278  1   40 
            double differential neutron emission spectrum in      22278  1   41 
            drastic disagreement with the measured one, the       22278  1   42 
            correction can be failed and the adoption of raw data 22278  1   43 
            is recommended by authors.                            22278  1   44 
COMMENT     Correction factor are calculated using evaluated data,22278  1   45 
            however, they are still primitive. Calculation of     22278  1   46 
            correction factors should be carried out again after  22278  1   47 
            new version of evaluation would be published.         22278  1   48
